<td style=" text-align: center;margin:auto; vertical-align:top"><ix:nonNumeric name="dei:Security12bTitle" contextRef="duration_2024-10-14_to_2024-10-14_us-gaap-StatementClassOfStockAxis_wba-M2.125WalgreensBootsAllianceInc.NotesDue2026Member" id="ixv-354">2.125% Walgreens Boots Alliance, Inc. notes due 2026</ix:nonNumeric></td>
<td style="vertical-align:bottom">&#160;</td>
<td style=" text-align: center;margin:auto; vertical-align:top"><ix:nonNumeric name="dei:TradingSymbol" contextRef="duration_2024-10-14_to_2024-10-14_us-gaap-StatementClassOfStockAxis_wba-M2.125WalgreensBootsAllianceInc.NotesDue2026Member" id="ixv-355">WBA26</ix:nonNumeric></td>
<td style="vertical-align:bottom">&#160;</td>
<td style=" text-align: center;margin:auto; vertical-align:top"><ix:nonNumeric name="dei:SecurityExchangeName" contextRef="duration_2024-10-14_to_2024-10-14_us-gaap-StatementClassOfStockAxis_wba-M2.125WalgreensBootsAllianceInc.NotesDue2026Member" format="ixt-sec:exchnameen" id="ixv-356">The Nasdaq Stock Market LLC</ix:nonNumeric></td></tr></table> <p style="margin-top:7pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Indicate by check mark whether the registrant is an emerging growth company as defined in Rule 405 of the Securities Act of 1933 (&#167;230.405 of this chapter) or Rule <span style="white-space:nowrap">12b-2</span> of the Securities Exchange Act of 1934 <span style="white-space:nowrap">(&#167;240.12b-2</span> of this chapter).</p> <p style="margin-top:7pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:right">Emerging growth company&#8194;<ix:nonNumeric name="dei:EntityEmergingGrowthCompany" contextRef="duration_2024-10-14_to_2024-10-14" format="ixt-sec:boolballotbox" id="ixv-357">&#9744;</ix:nonNumeric></p> <p style="margin-top:7pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">If an emerging growth company, indicate by check mark if the registrant has elected not to use the extended transition period for complying with any new or revised financial accounting standards provided pursuant to Section&#160;13(a) of the Exchange Act.&#8194;&#9744;</p> <p style="font-size:7pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&#160;</p> <p style="line-height:1.0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt;border-bottom:1px solid #000000">&#160;</p> <p style="line-height:3.0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:2pt;border-bottom:1px solid #000000">&#160;</p></div></div>

<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always"> </p>
<hr style="color:#999999;height:3px;width:100%;clear:both"/>

<div style="text-align:center"><div style="width:8.5in;text-align:left;margin-left: auto;margin-right: auto">
 <p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold"><span style="text-decoration:underline">Item</span>&#8201;<span style="text-decoration:underline">2.02</span>. <span style="text-decoration:underline">Results of Operations and Financial Condition</span>. </p> <p style="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">On October&#160;15, 2024, Walgreens Boots Alliance, Inc. (the &#8220;Company&#8221;) issued a press release announcing financial results for the fiscal quarter and fiscal year ended August&#160;31, 2024 and related matters. A copy of this press release is furnished as Exhibit 99.1 hereto and is incorporated in this Item 2.02 by reference. </p> <p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The information in this Item 2.02, including the exhibit attached hereto, and the information under Item 7.01 below, shall not be deemed &#8220;filed&#8221; for purposes of Section&#160;18 of the Securities Exchange Act of 1934, as amended (the &#8220;Exchange Act&#8221;), or otherwise subject to the liabilities of that section. This information shall not be deemed to be incorporated by reference in any filing under the Securities Act of 1933, as amended, or the Exchange Act, except as shall be expressly set forth by specific reference to such disclosure in this Form <span style="white-space:nowrap">8-K</span> in such a filing. </p> <p style="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold"><span style="text-decoration:underline">Item</span><span style="text-decoration:underline">&#8201;</span><span style="text-decoration:underline">2.05</span>. <span style="text-decoration:underline">Costs Associated with Exit or Disposal Activities</span>. </p> <p style="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">On October&#160;14, 2024, the Board of Directors of the Company approved a plan to optimize its footprint and close underperforming stores, primarily within the Company&#8217;s U.S. Retail Pharmacy segment (the &#8220;Footprint Optimization Program&#8221;). The Company believes that execution of this program will realign the Company&#8217;s footprint with evolving demographic trends and enhance its capacity to respond more effectively to shifts in consumer behavior and buying preferences. This increased agility in adapting to a changing environment is a key objective of the Company&#8217;s strategic review, and a critical area in which the Company aims to close the competitive gap with peers that have taken similar initiatives over the past years. The Company expects the economic benefits of this program will begin to be tangible in fiscal 2025. </p> <p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Footprint Optimization Program includes plans to close approximately 900 to 1,000 stores primarily across the U.S. by the end of fiscal 2027. The cadence of expected store closures prioritizes estimated cash flow benefits, underperforming locations, and lease expirations. The program is expected to be accretive to adjusted operating income and cash flows beginning in fiscal 2025, net of closure costs, with the possible benefits scaling as underlying leases expire. Including the remaining approximately 300 stores approved but not yet closed under the Transformational Cost Management Program, the Company expects to close an aggregate of 1,200 to 1,300 stores over the next three years, including approximately 500 stores projected to close in fiscal 2025. The Company also intends to follow its historic practice of redeploying the majority of the workforce in those stores that are closed. </p> <p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Company currently estimates that it will recognize cumulative <span style="white-space:nowrap">pre-tax</span> charges to its GAAP financial results of approximately $2.2&#160;billion to $2.4&#160;billion, including costs associated with lease obligations and other real estate costs, asset impairments, and employee severance and other exit costs. The Company expects to incur <span style="white-space:nowrap">pre-tax</span> charges of approximately $1.8&#160;billion to $2.0&#160;billion for lease obligations and other real estate costs including runoff costs associated with location optimization under prior programs, approximately $300&#160;million of asset impairments, and approximately $100&#160;million for employee severance and other exit costs. The Company estimates that approximately 90% of these cumulative <span style="white-space:nowrap">pre-tax</span> charges will result in future cash expenditures. </p> <p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The amounts and timing of all estimates are subject to change until finalized. The actual amounts and timing may vary materially based on various factors. See Part I, Item 1A Risk factors of our Form <span style="white-space:nowrap">10-K</span> for the fiscal year ended August&#160;31, 2023, as amended and &#8220;Cautionary Note Regarding Forward-Looking Statements&#8221; below. </p> <p style="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold"><span style="text-decoration:underline">Item</span>&#8201;<span style="text-decoration:underline">7.01</span>. <span style="text-decoration:underline">Regulation FD Disclosure</span>. </p> <p style="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">On October&#160;15, 2024, the Company is conducting a conference call and webcast beginning at 8:30 a.m. Eastern time regarding its results for the fiscal quarter and fiscal year ended August&#160;31, 2024 and related matters. </p> <p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Slides prepared for the purposes of the conference call are available on the Company&#8217;s investor relations website at http://investor.walgreensbootsalliance.com. A link to the conference call will be available on the Company&#8217;s investor relations website at: http://investor.walgreensbootsalliance.com. </p>
</div></div>



<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always"> </p>
<hr style="color:#999999;height:3px;width:100%;clear:both"/>

 <p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><span style="font-style:italic">Cautionary Note Regarding Forward-Looking Statements</span>: This current report on Form <span style="white-space:nowrap">8-K</span> contains forward-looking statements made pursuant to the safe harbor provisions of the Private Securities Litigation Reform Act of 1995. All statements in this current report on Form <span style="white-space:nowrap">8-K</span> that are not historical are forward-looking statements, including, without limitation, statements related to whether the Company will achieve the associated objectives with its Footprint Optimization Program, whether the costs and charges associated with optimization initiatives will exceed current estimates and forecasts, its ability to realize expected savings and benefits in the amounts and at the times anticipated, the timing of store closures, actual employee severance, asset impairments and other factors affecting inventory value, factors relating to real estate, including the timing and amount of sublease income and other lease expense, changes in management&#8217;s assumptions, including the Company&#8217;s ability to redeploy its existing workforce and performance and foot traffic of remaining stores, its ability to achieve anticipated financial results, risks associated with acquisitions, divestitures, joint ventures and strategic investments, outcomes of legal and regulatory matters, and changes in legislation or regulations. These forward-looking statements are not guarantees of future performance and are subject to risks, uncertainties and assumptions, known or unknown, including our ability to execute on the Footprint Optimization Program and the risks and uncertainties described in Item 1A (Risk Factors) of our Form <span style="white-space:nowrap">10-K</span> for the fiscal year ended August&#160;31, 2023, in Item 1A (Risk Factors) in our Quarterly Reports on Form <span style="white-space:nowrap">10-Q</span> and in other documents that we file or furnish with the Securities and Exchange Commission, that could cause actual results to vary materially from those indicated or anticipated. </p> <p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">We do not undertake, and expressly disclaim, any duty or obligation to update publicly any forward-looking statement after the date of this current report on Form <span style="white-space:nowrap">8-K,</span> whether as a result of new information, future events, changes in assumptions or otherwise. </p> <p style="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold"><span style="text-decoration:underline">Item</span><span style="text-decoration:underline">&#8201;</span><span style="text-decoration:underline">9.01</span>. <span style="text-decoration:underline">Financial Statements and Exhibits</span>. </p> <p style="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(d) <span style="text-decoration:underline">Exhibits</span> </p> <p style="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&#160;</p>

<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I>Fourth quarter financial results </I></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

to opioid liabilities recognized in prior periods, and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-cash</FONT> impairment charges for CareCentrix goodwill and equity investment in China </P></TD></TR></TABLE>

and litigation </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

27.9&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis, reflecting a challenging U.S. retail environment, net reimbursement pressure, lower sale-leaseback gains, and lapping the reversal of incentive accruals in the prior year, partly offset by cost savings
and improved profitability in the U.S. Healthcare segment </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

basis </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I>Strategic actions </I></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><I></I>Announcing footprint optimization program targeting approximately 1,200 closures<SUP
STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">3</SUP> over the next three years, including approximately 500 closures in fiscal 2025, which will be immediately accretive to adjusted EPS and free cash flow </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">DEERFIELD, Ill., Oct. 15,&nbsp;2024 &#151; Walgreens Boots Alliance, Inc. (Nasdaq: WBA) today announced financial results for the fiscal year and fourth
quarter that ended Aug. 31, 2024. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;Our financial results in the fiscal fourth quarter and full year 2024 reflected our disciplined execution on cost
management, working capital initiatives and capex reduction. In fiscal 2025, we are focusing on stabilizing the retail pharmacy by optimizing our footprint, controlling operating costs, improving cash flow, and continuing to address reimbursement
models to support dispensing margins and preserve patient access for the future,&#148; said Tim Wentworth, Chief Executive Officer, Walgreens Boots Alliance. &#147;Fiscal 2025 will be an important rebasing year as we advance our strategy<B> </B>to
drive value creation. This turnaround will take time, but we are confident it will yield significant financial and consumer benefits over the long term.&#148; </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Overview of Fourth Quarter Results </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">WBA fourth quarter
sales increased 6.0&nbsp;percent from the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter to $37.5&nbsp;billion, an increase of 6.1&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis, reflecting sales growth across all segments. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Fourth quarter operating loss was $978&nbsp;million, an increase of 117.1&nbsp;percent compared to the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT>
quarter. The increase in operating loss reflects a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-cash</FONT> goodwill impairment charge related to CareCentrix. Adjusted operating income<SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">2</SUP> was
$424&nbsp;million, a decrease of 37.7&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis, reflecting softer U.S. retail and pharmacy performance, lapping the reversal of incentive accruals and prior year sale-leaseback gains, partly offset by cost savings
initiatives and improved profitability in the U.S. Healthcare segment. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Net loss in the fourth quarter was $3.0&nbsp;billion compared to a net loss of
$180&nbsp;million in the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter, primarily driven by a higher operating loss, a $2.3&nbsp;billion <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-cash</FONT> charge for valuation allowance on deferred tax
assets primarily related to opioid liabilities recognized in prior periods, and a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-cash</FONT> impairment charge related to equity investment in China. Adjusted net earnings<SUP
STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">2</SUP> decreased 41.0&nbsp;percent to $340&nbsp;million, down 40.8&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis, reflecting lower adjusted operating income. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Loss per share was $3.48, compared to a loss per share of $0.21 in the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter. Adjusted EPS<SUP
STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">2</SUP> decreased 41.0&nbsp;percent to $0.39, reflecting a decrease of 40.8&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Net cash provided by operating activities was $1.3&nbsp;billion in the fourth quarter and free cash flow was $1.1&nbsp;billion, a $537&nbsp;million increase
compared with the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter, each driven primarily by working capital initiatives </P> <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">
 2
 </P>
</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always"> </p>
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">
and lower legal payments in the current period. Free cash flow also benefited from a $239&nbsp;million decrease in capital expenditures. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Overview of Fiscal Year Results </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Sales in fiscal 2024
were $147.7&nbsp;billion, an increase of 6.2&nbsp;percent from the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> period, and an increase of 5.7&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis, reflecting sales growth across all segments. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Operating loss in fiscal 2024 was $14.1&nbsp;billion, an increase of 104.5&nbsp;percent compared to the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT>
period. Operating loss in the current period reflects a $12.4&nbsp;billion <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-cash</FONT> impairment charge related to VillageMD goodwill, which resulted in a $5.8&nbsp;billion charge attributable to WBA, net of tax
and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-controlling</FONT> interest. Operating loss in the current period also reflects <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-cash</FONT> impairments charges related to certain long-lived assets in the U.S. Retail
Pharmacy segment and CareCentrix goodwill. Prior year operating loss reflects a $6.8&nbsp;billion <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pre-tax</FONT> charge for opioid-related claims and litigation and a $431&nbsp;million
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-cash</FONT> impairment of pharmacy license intangible assets in Boots UK. Adjusted operating income was $2.6&nbsp;billion, a decrease of 32.6&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis, reflecting a challenging
U.S. retail environment, net reimbursement pressure, lower sale-leaseback gains and lapping the reversal of incentive accruals in the prior year, partly offset by cost savings and improved profitability in the U.S. Healthcare segment. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Net loss in fiscal 2024 was $8.6&nbsp;billion, an increase of 180.4&nbsp;percent compared to the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> period,
primarily driven by a higher operating loss, a $2.2&nbsp;billion <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-cash</FONT> charge for valuation allowance on certain deferred tax assets and a $717&nbsp;million <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">after-tax</FONT>
charge for fair value adjustments on variable prepaid forward derivatives related to the monetization of Cencora shares. Adjusted net earnings<SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">2</SUP> were $2.5&nbsp;billion, a decrease of
27.9&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis, primarily driven by lower adjusted operating income, partly offset by lower interest expense and a lower adjusted effective tax rate due to the recognition of deferred tax assets in foreign
jurisdictions in the second quarter. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Loss per share for fiscal 2024 was $10.01, an increase of 180.4&nbsp;percent compared to the <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> period. Adjusted EPS<SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">2</SUP> was $2.88, a decrease of 27.6&nbsp;percent, reflecting a decrease of 27.9&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Net cash provided by operating activities was $1.0&nbsp;billion in fiscal 2024. Free cash flow<SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">2</SUP> was
$23&nbsp;million, a decrease of $642&nbsp;million from fiscal 2023, with each driven by lower earnings, higher payments related to legal matters and phasing of working capital. Free cash flow benefited from a $736&nbsp;million decrease in capital
expenditures. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Business Segments </B></P> <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P>

</TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The U.S. Retail Pharmacy segment had fourth quarter sales of $29.5&nbsp;billion, an increase of 6.5&nbsp;percent from the <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter. Comparable sales increased 8.3&nbsp;percent from the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Pharmacy sales increased 9.6&nbsp;percent and comparable pharmacy sales increased 11.7&nbsp;percent in the fourth quarter, each driven by higher brand
inflation and mix impacts. Comparable prescriptions, adjusted to <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">30-day</FONT> equivalents increased 2.5&nbsp;percent and comparable prescriptions excluding immunizations increased 2.6&nbsp;percent compared with the <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter. Total prescriptions filled in the quarter, including immunizations, adjusted to <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">30-day</FONT> equivalents, increased 1.7&nbsp;percent to 302&nbsp;million. Pharmacy
margin was negatively impacted by net reimbursement pressure, brand inflation and mix impacts. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Retail sales decreased 3.5&nbsp;percent and comparable
retail sales decreased 1.7&nbsp;percent compared with the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter, reflecting a challenging retail environment and continued channel shift. Retail margin was positively impacted by category mix and
higher owned brand penetration, partly offset by elevated shrink levels. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Adjusted operating income<SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">4</SUP>
decreased 60.4&nbsp;percent to $220&nbsp;million, reflecting net reimbursement pressure, a $123&nbsp;million headwind from a prior year incentive accrual release, a $74&nbsp;million headwind from lower sale-leaseback gains and a challenging retail
environment, partly offset by cost savings initiatives. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>International </B></P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

</TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The International segment had fourth quarter sales of $6.0&nbsp;billion, an increase of 3.2&nbsp;percent from the <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter. Sales increased 3.7&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis, with the Germany wholesale business sales growing 8.2&nbsp;percent and Boots UK sales growing 2.3&nbsp;percent. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Boots UK comparable pharmacy sales increased 10.0&nbsp;percent compared with the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter. Comparable retail
sales increased 6.2&nbsp;percent compared to the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter, with growth across all categories. Boots.com continued to perform strongly with sales growing 19&nbsp;percent, representing 15&nbsp;percent of
Boots total retail sales. </P> <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">

in the prior year period, reflecting the $332&nbsp;million <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-cash</FONT> goodwill impairment charge related to CareCentrix. Adjusted operating income<SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">4</SUP>, which
excludes certain costs related to stock compensation expense and amortization of acquired intangible assets, was $17&nbsp;million compared to an adjusted operating loss of $83&nbsp;million in the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT>
quarter. Adjusted EBITDA<SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">2</SUP> of $65&nbsp;million improved by $94&nbsp;million versus the prior year quarter, driven by cost discipline at VillageMD and growth from Shields. </P>

<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">ENDS </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:24pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>Notes to Editors:
</B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>About Walgreens Boots Alliance </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Walgreens Boots
Alliance (Nasdaq: WBA) is an integrated healthcare, pharmacy and retail leader serving millions of customers and patients every day, with a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">170-year</FONT> heritage of caring for communities. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">A trusted, global innovator in retail pharmacy with approximately 12,500 locations across the U.S., Europe and Latin America, WBA plays a critical role in the
healthcare ecosystem. The company is reimagining local healthcare and well-being for all as part of its purpose. Through dispensing medicines, improving access to a wide range of </P>
<p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">
 7
 </P>
</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always"> </p>
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">
health services, providing high quality health and beauty products and offering anytime, anywhere convenience across its digital platforms, WBA is shaping the future of healthcare. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">WBA employs approximately 312,000 people and has a presence in eight countries through its portfolio of consumer brands: Walgreens, Boots, Duane Reade, the
No7 Beauty Company and Benavides in Mexico. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Additionally, WBA has a portfolio of healthcare-focused investments located in several countries, including
China and the U.S. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Company is proud of its contributions to healthy communities, a healthy planet, an inclusive workplace and a sustainable
marketplace. WBA has been recognized for its commitment to being an inclusive workplace. In fiscal 2024, the Company scored 100% on the Disability Equality Index for disability inclusion. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">More Company information is available at <U>www.walgreensbootsalliance.com</U>. </P>

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>WALGREENS BOOTS ALLIANCE, INC. AND SUBSIDIARIES </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>SUPPLEMENTAL INFORMATION (UNAUDITED) </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>REGARDING <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">NON-GAAP</FONT> FINANCIAL MEASURES </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The following information provides reconciliations of the supplemental <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures, as defined under
the SEC rules, presented in this press release to the most directly comparable financial measures calculated and presented in accordance with generally accepted accounting principles in the United States (GAAP). The Company has provided the <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures in the press release, which are not calculated or presented in accordance with GAAP, as supplemental information and in addition to the financial measures that are calculated and
presented in accordance with GAAP. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">These supplemental <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures are presented because
management has evaluated the Company&#146;s financial results both including and excluding the adjusted items or the effects of foreign currency translation, as applicable, and believes that the supplemental
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures presented provide additional perspective and insights when analyzing the core operating performance of the Company from period to period and trends in the Company&#146;s historical
operating results. The Company also uses <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures as a basis for certain compensation programs it sponsors. These supplemental <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial
measures should not be considered superior to, as a substitute for or as an alternative to, and should be considered in conjunction with, the GAAP financial measures presented in the press release. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Company does not provide a reconciliation for <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> estimates to the most directly comparable GAAP financial
measures on a forward-looking basis where it is unable to provide a meaningful or accurate calculation or estimation of reconciling items and the information is not available without unreasonable effort. This is due to the inherent difficulty of
forecasting the timing or amount of various items that have not yet occurred, are out of the Company&#146;s control and/or cannot be reasonably predicted, such as unusual <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">one-time</FONT> charges, tax expenses, and
material litigation expenses, and that would impact diluted net earnings per share, the most directly comparable forward-looking GAAP financial measure. For the same reasons, the Company is unable to address the probable significance of the
unavailable information. Forward-looking <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures provided without the most directly comparable GAAP financial measures may vary materially from the corresponding GAAP financial measures.
</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I>Constant currency </I></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Company also presents certain
information related to current period operating results in &#147;constant currency,&#148; which is a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measure. These amounts are calculated by translating current period results at the
foreign currency exchange rates used in the comparable period in the prior year. The Company presents such constant currency financial information because it has significant operations outside of the U.S. reporting in currencies other than the U.S.
dollar and such presentation provides a framework to assess how its business performed excluding the impact of foreign currency exchange rate fluctuations. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I>Comparable sales </I></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The twelve months ended August&nbsp;31,
2024 comparable sales and prescriptions filled figures for the Company exclude the benefit of this year&#146;s leap day. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">13 </P>

</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always"> </p>
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">For the Company&#146;s U.S. Retail Pharmacy and International segments, Comparable sales are defined as
sales from stores that have been open for at least twelve consecutive months without closure for seven or more consecutive days, including due to looting or store damage, and without a major remodel or being subject to a natural disaster, in the
past twelve months as well as <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">e-commerce</FONT> sales. Comparable sales in constant currency exclude wholesale </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">sales in
Germany and sales from dispositions in the current period. <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">E-commerce</FONT> sales include digitally initiated sales online or through mobile applications. Relocated stores are not included as comparable sales for
the first twelve months after the relocation. Acquired stores are not included as comparable sales for the first twelve months after acquisition or conversion, when applicable, whichever is later. Comparable sales, comparable pharmacy sales,
comparable retail sales, comparable number of prescriptions and comparable number of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">30-day</FONT> equivalent prescriptions refer to total sales, pharmacy sales, retail sales, number of prescriptions and number of <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">30-day</FONT> equivalent prescriptions, respectively. The method of calculating comparable sales varies across the retail industry and our method of calculating comparable sales may not be the same as other retailers&#146;
methods. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">With respect to the International segment, comparable sales, comparable pharmacy sales and comparable retail sales, are presented on a constant
currency basis, which is a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measure. Refer to the discussion above in &#147;Constant currency&#148; for further details on constant currency calculations. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I>Key Performance Indicators </I></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Company considers certain
metrics, such as comparable sales (in constant currency), comparable pharmacy sales (in constant currency), comparable retail sales (in constant currency), comparable number of prescriptions, and comparable
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">30-day</FONT> equivalent prescriptions to be key performance indicators because the Company&#146;s management has evaluated its results of operations using these metrics and believes that these key performance
indicators presented provide additional perspective and insights when analyzing the core operating performance of the Company from period to period and trends in its historical operating results. These key performance indicators should not be
considered superior to, as a substitute for or as an alternative to, and should be considered in conjunction with, the GAAP financial measures presented herein. These measures may not be comparable to similarly-titled performance indicators used by
other companies. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">14 </P>

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">

<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">1</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">In the second quarter of fiscal 2024, the Company recorded $12.4&nbsp;billion of
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-cash</FONT> impairment charges related to VillageMD goodwill. In the fourth quarter of fiscal 2024, the Company recorded $332&nbsp;million of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-cash</FONT> impairment charges
related to CareCentrix goodwill. These charges are recorded within Selling, general and administrative expenses and Impairment of goodwill within the Consolidated Statements of Earnings. In fiscal 2023, the Company recognized a $431&nbsp;million
impairment of pharmacy license intangible assets in Boots UK of which $132&nbsp;million was attributed to additional store closures recognized as part of the Transformational Cost Management Program. These charges are recorded within Selling,
general and administrative expenses within the Consolidated Statements of Earnings. The Company excludes these charges when evaluating operating performance because it does not incur such charges on a predictable basis and exclusion of such charges
enables more consistent evaluation of the Company&#146;s operating performance. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">2</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Certain legal and regulatory accruals and settlements relate to significant charges associated with certain
legal proceedings, including legal defense costs. The Company excludes these charges when evaluating operating performance because it does not incur such charges on a predictable basis and exclusion of such charges enables more consistent evaluation
of the Company&#146;s operating performance. These charges are recorded in Selling, general and administrative expenses within the Consolidated Statements of Earnings. In fiscal 2024 and 2023, the Company recorded charges related to the opioid
litigation Multistate Agreement and certain other legal matters. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">3</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Transformational Cost Management Program charges are costs associated with a formal restructuring plan. These
charges are primarily recorded in Selling, general and administrative expenses within the Consolidated Statements of Earnings. These costs do not reflect current operating performance and are impacted by the timing of restructuring activity.
</P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">4</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Acquisition-related amortization includes amortization of acquisition-related intangible assets and stock-based
compensation fair valuation adjustments. Amortization of acquisition-related intangible assets includes amortization of intangible assets such as customer relationships, trade names, trademarks, developed technology and contract intangibles.
Intangible asset amortization excluded from the related <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measure represents the entire amount recorded within the Company&#146;s GAAP financial statements. The revenue generated by the associated
intangible assets has not been excluded from the related <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measures. Amortization expense, unlike the related revenue, is not affected by operations of any particular period unless an intangible asset
becomes impaired, or the estimated useful life of an intangible asset is revised. These charges are primarily recorded in Selling, general and administrative expenses within the Consolidated Statements of Earnings. The stock-based compensation fair
valuation adjustment reflects the difference between the fair value based remeasurement of awards under purchase accounting and the grant date fair valuation. Post-acquisition compensation expense recognized in excess of the original grant date fair
value of acquiree awards are excluded from the related <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measures as these arise from acquisition-related accounting requirements or agreements, and are not reflective of normal operating activities.
</P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">5</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Acquisition-related costs are transaction and integration costs associated with certain merger, acquisition and
divestitures related activities recorded in Operating (loss) income within the Consolidated Statements of Earnings. Examples of such costs include deal costs, severance, stock-based compensation, employee transaction success bonuses, and other
integration related exit and disposal charges. These charges are primarily recorded within Selling, general and administrative expenses within the Consolidated Statements of Earnings. These costs are significantly impacted by the timing and
complexity of the underlying merger, acquisition and divestitures related activities and do not reflect the Company&#146;s current operating performance. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">6</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Adjustments to equity earnings in Cencora consist of the Company&#146;s proportionate share of <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> adjustments reported by Cencora consistent with the Company&#146;s <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measures. Adjustments are recorded to equity earnings in Cencora within the Consolidated
Statements of Earnings. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">7</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">The Company&#146;s U.S. Retail Pharmacy segment inventory is accounted for using the <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">last-in-first-out</FONT></FONT></FONT> (&#147;LIFO&#148;) method. This adjustment represents the impact on cost of sales as if the U.S. Retail Pharmacy
segment inventory is accounted for using <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">first-in</FONT> <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">first-out</FONT> (&#147;FIFO&#148;) method. The LIFO provision is affected by changes in inventory quantities, product mix,
and manufacturer pricing practices, which may be impacted by market and other external influences. Therefore, the Company cannot control the amounts recognized or timing of these items. These charges are recorded within Cost of sales within the
Consolidated Statements of Earnings. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">8</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Store damage and inventory loss insurance recovery for losses incurred in fiscal 2020 as a result of looting in
the U.S. These charges are primarily recorded within Selling, general and administrative expenses within the Consolidated Statements of Earnings. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">9</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Impairment of equity method investment and investments in debt and equity securities includes impairment of
certain investments. The Company excludes these charges when evaluating operating performance because these do not relate to the ordinary course of the Company&#146;s business and it does not incur such charges on a predictable basis. Exclusion of
such charges enables more consistent evaluation of the Company&#146;s operating performance. These charges are recorded within Other income, net, in the Consolidated Statements of Earnings. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>

the Consolidated Statements of Earnings. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Includes fair value gains or losses on the VPF derivatives and certain derivative instruments used as economic
hedges of the Company&#146;s net investments in foreign subsidiaries. These charges are recorded within Other income, net, in the Consolidated Statements of Earnings. The Company does not believe this volatility related to the <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-cash</FONT> <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">mark-to-market</FONT></FONT> adjustments on the underlying derivative instruments reflects the Company&#146;s operational performance.
</P></TD></TR></TABLE>

adjustments recorded on investments in equity securities to Other income, net, in the Consolidated Statements of Earnings. In fiscal 2023, the Company recorded <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pre-tax</FONT> gains of $109&nbsp;million related to the
change in classification of its previously held equity method investment in Option Care Health to an investment in equity security held at fair value and subsequent related fair value adjustments. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>

complete the Trustee&#146;s acquisition of a bulk annuity policy (the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">&#147;Buy-In&#148;)</FONT> from Legal&nbsp;&amp; General. The payments and related incremental interest expense are not indicative of normal
operating performance. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">15</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">In fiscal 2024, the Company recorded a $2.2&nbsp;billion <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-cash</FONT>
charge due to recognition of a valuation allowance against certain U.S. and state deferred tax assets primarily related to opioid liabilities recognized in prior periods. Adjustments to income tax provision (benefit) include adjustments to the GAAP
basis tax provision (benefit) commensurate with <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> adjustments and certain discrete tax items including U.S. and UK tax law changes and equity method <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-cash</FONT> tax.
These charges are recorded within Income tax provision (benefit) within the Consolidated Statements of Earnings. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">16</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Adjustments to <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">post-tax</FONT> earnings from other equity method investments
consist of the proportionate share of certain equity method investees&#146; <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-cash</FONT> items or unusual or infrequent items consistent with the Company&#146;s <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT>
adjustments. These charges are recorded in <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Post-tax</FONT> earnings from other equity method investments within the Consolidated Statements of Earnings. Although the Company may have shareholder rights and board
representation commensurate with its ownership interests in these equity method investees, adjustments relating to equity method investments are not intended to imply that the Company has direct control over their operations and resulting revenue
and expenses. Moreover, these <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures have limitations in that they do not reflect all revenue and expenses of these equity method investees. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Due to the anti-dilutive effect resulting from periods where the Company reports a net loss, the impact of
potentially dilutive securities on the per share amounts has been omitted from the calculation of weighted-average common shares outstanding for diluted net loss per common share. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>

diluted for adjusted diluted net earnings per common share calculation purposes. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">The Company reconciles Adjusted EBITDA for the U.S. Healthcare segment to Operating loss as the closest GAAP
measure for the segment profitability. The Company does not measure Net earnings attributable to Walgreens Boots Alliance, Inc. for its segments. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">2</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">In the second quarter of fiscal 2024, the Company recorded $12.4&nbsp;billion of
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-cash</FONT> impairment charges related to VillageMD goodwill. In the fourth quarter of fiscal 2024, the Company recorded $332&nbsp;million of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-cash</FONT> impairment charges
related to CareCentrix goodwill. These charges are recorded within Selling, general and administrative expenses and Impairment of goodwill within the Consolidated Statements of Earnings. The Company excludes these charges when evaluating operating
performance because it does not incur such charges on a predictable basis and exclusion of such charges enables more consistent evaluation of the Company&#146;s operating performance. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">3</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Acquisition-related amortization includes amortization of acquisition-related intangible assets and stock-based
compensation fair valuation adjustments. Amortization of acquisition-related intangible assets includes amortization of intangible assets such as customer relationships, trade names, trademarks, developed technology and contract intangibles.
Intangible asset amortization excluded from the related <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measure represents the entire amount recorded within the Company&#146;s GAAP financial statements. The revenue generated by the associated
intangible assets has not been excluded from the related <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measures. Amortization expense, unlike the related revenue, is not affected by operations of any particular period unless an intangible asset
becomes impaired, or the estimated useful life of an intangible asset is revised. These charges are primarily recorded in Selling, general and administrative expenses within the Consolidated Statements of Earnings. The stock-based compensation fair
valuation adjustment reflects the difference between the fair value based remeasurement of awards under purchase accounting and the grant date fair valuation. Post-acquisition compensation expense recognized in excess of the original grant date fair
value of acquiree awards are excluded from the related <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measures as these arise from acquisition-related accounting requirements or agreements, and are not reflective of normal operating activities.
</P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">4</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Acquisition-related costs are transaction and integration costs associated with certain merger, acquisition and
divestitures related activities recorded in Operating (loss) income within the Consolidated Statements of Earnings. Examples of such costs include deal costs, severance, stock-based compensation, employee transaction success bonuses, and other
integration related exit and disposal charges. These charges are primarily recorded within Selling, general and administrative expenses within the Consolidated Statements of Earnings. These costs are significantly impacted by the timing and
complexity of the underlying merger, acquisition and divestitures related activities and do not reflect the Company&#146;s current operating performance. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">5</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Transformational Cost Management Program charges are costs associated with a formal restructuring plan. These
charges are primarily recorded in Selling, general and administrative expenses within the Consolidated Statements of Earnings. These costs do not reflect current operating performance and are impacted by the timing of restructuring activity.
</P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">6</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Includes GAAP stock-based compensation expense excluding expenses related to acquisition-related amortization
and acquisition-related costs. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">22 </P>

</DIV></Center>

<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">1</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Free cash flow is defined as net cash provided by operating activities in a period less additions to property,
plant and equipment (capital expenditures), plus acquisition related payments and incremental pension payments made in that period. This measure does not represent residual cash flows available for discretionary expenditures as the measure does not
deduct the payments required for debt service and other contractual obligations or payments for future business acquisitions. Therefore, we believe it is important to view free cash flow as a measure that provides supplemental information to the
Consolidated Statement of Cash Flows. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">2</SUP></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">In fiscal 2023, the Company paid $335&nbsp;million to settle liability classified share-based payment awards
related to acquiring the remaining 30% equity interest in Shields, $101&nbsp;million to settle liability classified share-based payment awards related to acquiring the remaining 45% equity interest in CareCentrix, and also <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">one-time</FONT> compensation costs related to VillageMD&#146;s acquisition of Summit. These payments are not indicative of normal operating performance. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">3</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">In fiscal 2024, the Company made incremental pension contributions of $386M to the Boots Plan as part of the
Trustee&#146;s acquisition of a bulk annuity policy (the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">&#147;Buy-In&#148;)</FONT> from Legal and General. The payments are not indicative of normal operating performance. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
